        ]
        analytics.factory = function (e) {
          return function () {
            var t = Array.prototype.slice.call(arguments)
            t.unshift(e)
            analytics.push(t)
            return analytics
          }
        }
        for (var e = 0; e < analytics.methods.length; e++) {

          analytics[key] = analytics.factory(key)

    <script data-ot-ignore>
  const SEGMENT_DATA = {
    customer: {
      id: '',
      email: '',
      first_name: '',
      last_name: '',
    },
  }

  window.Segment = {
    debug: Boolean(localStorage && localStorage.getItem('segment.debug')),

    init() {},

    centsToMoney(cents) {
      return ((parseFloat(`${cents}`) || 0) / 100).toFixed(2)
    },

    getContext() {
      const email = SEGMENT_DATA.customer.email

      return email
        ? {
            externalIds: [
              {
                id: SEGMENT_DATA.customer.email,
                type: 'email',
                collection: 'users',
                encoding: 'none',
              },
            ],
          }
        : {}
    },

    getTargetingCookiesAllowed() {
      const reduceQueryToObject = (object, part) => {
        const [key, ...values] = part.split(/\s*=\s*/)
        object[key] = decodeURIComponent(values.join('='))
        return object
      }
      const cookies = document.cookie
        .split(/\s*;\s*/)
        .reduce(reduceQueryToObject, {})

      const consentCookie = cookies.OptanonConsent || null
      if (!consentCookie) return true

      const consentData = consentCookie
        .split('&')
        .reduce(reduceQueryToObject, {})
      if (!consentData) return false

      const groups = consentData.groups || null
      const targetingCookieGroup = 'C0004'

      return groups ? groups.includes(`${targetingCookieGroup}:1`) : false
    },

    validate() {
      if (!this.getTargetingCookiesAllowed()) {
        console.warn('Analytics not allowed')
        return false
      }

      if (typeof window.analytics === 'undefined') {
        console.warn('Analytics not enabled')
        return false
      }

      return true
    },

    async getUser() {
      if (!this.validate()) {
        return null
      }

      return await new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
        analytics.ready(() => {
          resolve(analytics.user())
        })
      })
    },

    track(event, properties = {}) {
      if (!this.validate()) return

      this.debugTrack(event, properties)
      analytics.track(event, properties, this.getContext())
    },

    debugTrack(event, properties = {}) {
      if (!this.debug) return

      console.log(`Analytics event fired`, {
        event,
        properties,
      })
    },

    identify(userId = null, traits) {
      if (!this.validate()) return

      this.debugIdentify(userId, traits)

      if (userId) {
        analytics.identify(userId, traits)
      } else {
        analytics.identify(traits)
      }
    },

    debugIdentify(userId, traits) {
      if (!this.debug) return

      console.log(`Analytics identify fired`, {
        userId,
        traits,
      })
    },

    alias(customerId, previousId) {
      if (!this.validate()) return

      this.debugAlias(userId, previousId)

      analytics.alias(userId, previousId)
    },

    debugAlias(userId, previousId) {
      if (!this.debug) return

      console.log(`Analytics alias fired`, {
        userId,
        previousId,
      })
    },
  }

  window.onload = Segment.init()
</script>

<script>
Vue.component('cart-modal', {
  template: '#cart-modal',

  props: {
    open: Boolean,
    cartAccessories: Array,
  },

  delimiters: ['${', '}'],

  data() {
    return {
      loading: false,
      cart: CartJS.cart,
      tmpScrollTop: 0,
      mobileModes: {
        ITEMS: 0,
        SUGGESTED: 1,
      },
      mobileMode: 0,
      expandedProductIds: [],
      wasQuantityReduced: false,
      Shopify
    };
  },

  computed: {
    /**
     * @returns {Object}
     */
    customer() {
      return this.$root.appData.customer;
    },

    /**
     * Cart items shortcut, always returns an array
     *
     * @returns {Array}
     */
    cartItems() {
      return this.cart.items || [];
    },

    /**
     * Check if there are items in the cart
     *
     * @returns {boolean}
     */
    isCartEmpty() {
      return this.cartItems.length === 0;
    },

    /**
     * Get suggested products
     *
     * @returns {Array}
     */
    suggestedProducts() {
      // Return no products if the cart is empty - do not suggest anything
      if (this.isCartEmpty) {
        return [];
      }

      // Clone the accessories
      let accessories = this.cartAccessories.slice(0);

      // Sort based on the priority
      accessories = accessories.sort(
        (a, b) => parseFloat(b.data.priority || 1) - parseFloat(a.data.priority || 1),
      );

      return accessories;
    },

    /**
     * Get suggested product variants that are available
     *
     * @returns {Array}
     */
    suggestedVariants() {
      let variants = [];
      const maxVariantCount = 15;

      const checkView = viewData => {
        // Legacy boolean value
        if (!Array.isArray(viewData)) {
          return false;
        }

        // Ignored SKU not in cart
        if (viewData.some(sku => this.cartItems.some(item => item.sku === `!${sku}`))) {
          return false;
        }

        // Wildcard
        if (viewData.includes('*')) {
          return true;
        }

        // SKU in cart
        return viewData.some(sku => this.cartItems.some(item => item.sku === sku));
      };

      for (const product of this.suggestedProducts) {
        for (const variant of product.variants) {
          const isInCart = this.cartItems.some(
            item => item.sku === variant.sku,
          );

          // Add product object reference to the variant
          variant.product = product;

          // Add the variant to the list if not already in the cart
          if (!isInCart) {
            variants.push(variant);
          }
        }
      }

      // Hide variants that are not allowed for cart items
      variants = variants.filter(variant => {
        const data = variant.product.data || {};
        const dataFor = data.for || {};

        const checkFor = (dataKey, itemKey) => {
          if (dataFor[dataKey] && dataFor[dataKey].length) {
            let found = false;

            dataFor[dataKey].forEach(value => {
              if (this.cartItems.some(item => item[itemKey] === value)) {
                found = true;
                return;
              }
            });

            // Valid if targetted product is found in the cart
            return found;
          }

          // Valid by default
          return true;
        };

        // Check the country validity
        if (
          Array.isArray(data.countries) &&
          data.countries.length &&
          !data.countries.includes('US')
        ) {
          return false;
        }

        // Check for product match
        if (data.view && data.view.checkout && !checkView(data.view.checkout)) {
          return false;
        }

        // Lastly, check for targetted products
        return (
          checkFor('product-vendors', 'vendor') &&
          checkFor('product-types', 'product_type')
        );
      });

      // Limit variant count
      variants.splice(maxVariantCount);

      return variants;
    },

    /**
     * Check for suggested product count
     *
     * @returns {boolean}
     */
    hasSuggestedProducts() {
      return this.suggestedProducts.length > 0;
    },

    /**
     * Check for suggested product variant count
     *
     * @returns {boolean}
     */
    hasSuggestedVariants() {
      return this.suggestedVariants.length > 0;
    },

    /**
     * Check if accented sections should be shown
     *
     * @returns {boolean}
     */
    showAccented() {
      return (
        !this.$root.isMobileResolution ||
        this.mobileMode === this.mobileModes.ITEMS
      );
    },
  },

  methods: {
    /**
     * Toggle suggested product variant collapsing
     *
     * @param {number} productId
     */
    toggleSuggestedProduct(productId) {
      const expandedProductIndex = this.expandedProductIds.indexOf(productId);

      if (expandedProductIndex === -1) {
        // Expand
        this.expandedProductIds.push(productId);
      } else {
        // Collapse
        this.expandedProductIds.splice(expandedProductIndex, 1);
      }
    },

    /**
     * Check if the product is expanded
     *
     * @param {number} productId
     * @returns {Boolean}
     */
    suggestedProductExpanded(productId) {
      return this.expandedProductIds.includes(productId);
    },

    /**
     * Check to see if the suggested variant can be shown
     *
     * @param {Object} variant
     * @returns {boolean}
     */
    canShowSuggestedVariant(variant) {
      return this.suggestedVariants.some(({ sku }) => sku === variant.sku);
    },

    /**
     * Filter suggested product variants that can be shown
     *
     * @param {Object} product
     * @returns {Array}
     */
    productSuggestedVariants(product) {
      return product.variants.filter(this.canShowSuggestedVariant);
    },

    /**
     * Set the current mobile mode
     *
     * @param {number} mode
     */
    setMobileMode(mode) {
      this.mobileMode = mode;
    },

    /**
     * Parse the variant and build a title
     *
     * @param {Object} variant
     * @returns {string}
     */
    getVariantTitle(variant) {
      let title = variant.product.title;

      if (variant.title !== 'Default Title') {
        title += ` - ${variant.title}`;
      }

      return title;
    },

    /**
     * Send a custom close event for the parent to handle
     */
    closeModal() {
      this.$emit('close');
    },

    /**
     * Enable loading when the cart is about to update
     */
    onBeforeCartUpdate() {
      this.loading = true;
    },

    /**
     * Update component data on cart update
     *
     * @param {Object} event
     * @param {Object} cart
     */
    onCartUpdate(event, cart) {
      // Update the cart data
      this.cart = cart;
      this.loading = false;
    },

    /**
     * Validate cart quantities
     * Attribute are set in vue-product-cart-relations
     */
    async checkCartProductQuantities() {
      const { items } = this.cart;
      const limitsAttribute = this.$root.getCartAttribute('quantity-limits');
      const kitsAttribute = this.$root.getCartAttribute('quantity-kits');
      const hddsAttribute = this.$root.getCartAttribute('quantity-hdds');

      const itemQuantities = {};
      const debugQuantityChanges = false;
      const setItemQuantity = (itemId, quantity, reason = '') => {
        if (debugQuantityChanges) {
          console.log(`${itemId} was set as ${quantity}`, reason ? `: ${reason}` : '');
        }
        itemQuantities[itemId] = quantity;
      };

      // Manage HDDs
      const cartHddIdMaxQties = {};
      const allCartHddIds = [];

      for (const [dependantProductId, hdds] of Object.entries(hddsAttribute)) {
        const dependantCartItem = items.find(
          ({ product_id: productId }) =>
            `${productId}` === `${dependantProductId}`,
        );
        const hddSkus = Object.values(hdds).map(({ sku }) => sku);

        items
          .filter(({ sku }) => hddSkus.includes(sku))
          .forEach(({ id, sku }) => {
            // Store the HDD id
            if (!allCartHddIds.includes(id)) {
              allCartHddIds.push(id);
            }

            // Set the max allowed quantity if possible
            if (dependantCartItem) {
              const hdd = Object.values(hdds).find(hdd => hdd.sku === sku);
              const prevQty = parseInt(cartHddIdMaxQties[id]) || 0;
              const dependantQty = parseInt(dependantCartItem.quantity);
              const ratio = (hdd && parseInt(hdd.ratio)) || 1;

              cartHddIdMaxQties[id] = prevQty + dependantQty * ratio;
            }
          });
      }

      for (const cartHddId of allCartHddIds) {
        const cartHdd = items.find(({ id }) => `${id}` === `${cartHddId}`);
        const cartHddMaxQty = parseInt(cartHddIdMaxQties[cartHddId]) || 0;

        if (cartHdd && cartHdd.quantity > cartHddMaxQty) {
          // Limit the allowed max quantity
          setItemQuantity(cartHddId, cartHddMaxQty, 'HDD max limit');
        }
      }

      // Manage kits
      for (const [parentProductId, kitItems] of Object.entries(kitsAttribute)) {
        const parentCartItem = items.find(
          ({ product_id: productId }) =>
            `${productId}` === `${parentProductId}`,
        );
        const parentProductLimits = limitsAttribute[parentProductId];

        if (parentCartItem) {
          for (const kitItem of Object.values(kitItems)) {
            // Add the kit item to the cart if not there already
            if (!items.some(({ id }) => `${id}` === `${kitItem.itemId}`)) {
              const quantity = parseInt(kitItem.quantity) || 1;

              setItemQuantity(kitItem.itemId, quantity * parentCartItem.quantity, 'Kit item');
            }
          }

          // Remove the parent item from cart
          setItemQuantity(parentCartItem.id, 0, 'Kit parent item');
        } else {
          // Check and manage the cart kit items
          const kitItemIds = Object.values(kitItems).map(
            ({ itemId }) => `${itemId}`,
          );
          const kitCartItems = items.filter(({ id }) =>
            kitItemIds.includes(`${id}`),
          );

          if (kitCartItems.length < kitItemIds.length) {
            // Remove dangling kit items
            for (const kitItem of Object.values(kitItems)) {
              if (
                kitCartItems.some(({ id }) => `${id}` === `${kitItem.itemId}`)
              ) {
                setItemQuantity(kitItem.itemId, 0, 'Dangling kit item');
              }
            }
          } else {
            // Manage kit item quantity linking
            const kitCartQties = kitCartItems.map(({ quantity }) =>
              parseInt(quantity),
            );
            const kitCartQtiesUnique = [...new Set(kitCartQties)];

            if (kitCartQtiesUnique.length > 1) {
              const quantity = this.wasQuantityReduced
                ? Math.min(...kitCartQtiesUnique)
                : Math.max(...kitCartQtiesUnique);

              for (const kitItemId of kitItemIds) {
                setItemQuantity(kitItemId, quantity, 'Equalize kit item quantities');
              }
            }
          }
        }

        // Adjust the quantity limits based on the parent
        if (parentProductLimits) {
          const { minimum, maximum } = parentProductLimits;

          for (const { itemId } of Object.values(kitItems)) {
            const quantity = itemQuantities[itemId];

            if (maximum && quantity > maximum) {
              setItemQuantity(itemId, maximum, 'Max allowed parent qty');
            } else if (minimum && quantity < minimum) {
              setItemQuantity(itemId, minimum, 'Min allowed parent qty');
            }
          }
        }
      }

      // Manage limits - has to be the last one
      for (const [limitProductId, limits] of Object.entries(limitsAttribute)) {
        const minimum = parseInt(limits.minimum) || this.$root.defaultQtyMinimum;
        const maximum = parseInt(limits.maximum) || this.$root.defaultQtyMaximum;
        const multiple = parseInt(limits.multiple) || null;

        for (const item of items) {
          const { id, product_id: productId } = item;
          let { quantity } = item

          if (`${productId}` === `${limitProductId}`) {
            // Enforce step - has to be the first one
            if (multiple !== null && multiple >= 0 && quantity % multiple !== 0) {
              const diff = quantity % multiple;
              const additive = this.wasQuantityReduced ? -diff : multiple - diff;

              quantity += additive;
              setItemQuantity(id, quantity, 'Multi step quantity');
            }

            // Enforce max quantity
            if (maximum !== null && maximum >= 0 && quantity > maximum) {
              setItemQuantity(id, maximum, 'Max allowed qty');
            }

            // Enforce min quantity
            if (minimum !== null && minimum >= 0 && quantity < minimum) {
              // Allow setting it to 0 always
              setItemQuantity(id, quantity > 0 ? minimum : 0, 'Min allowed quantity');
            }
          }
        }
      }

      // Per-customer limits
      const customerProductLimits = await this.$root.getCustomerProductLimits();

      if (customerProductLimits) {
        const notLoggedIn = !(this.customer.email && this.customer.email.length);
        const boughtItemQties = this.$root.getBoughtItemQtiesGroupedBySku();

        for (const item of items) {
          const { id, quantity } = item;
          const variantMaxQtyLimit = customerProductLimits.find(
            limit => limit.sku.toLowerCase() === item.sku.toLowerCase()
          );

          if (!variantMaxQtyLimit) {
            continue;
          }

          if (notLoggedIn) {
            // Set the item quantity to 0 due to requiring a login
            setItemQuantity(id, 0, 'Customer product limits requires logging in');
            continue;
          }

          const boughtQty = boughtItemQties[item.sku] || 0;
          const customerAllowedQty = variantMaxQtyLimit.max - boughtQty;

          if (quantity > customerAllowedQty) {
            // Update the item quantity to the allowed limit
            const finalItemQty = customerAllowedQty >= 0 ? customerAllowedQty : 0;

            setItemQuantity(id, finalItemQty, 'Customer product limits max allowed');
          }
        }
      }

      // Update quantities
      if (Object.values(itemQuantities).length) {
        // If any product is sold out or fails, all updates are cancelled so it's individual updates
        for (const [itemId, quantity] of Object.entries(itemQuantities)) {
          if (/^[0-9]+$/.test(quantity)) {
            CartJS.updateItemQuantitiesById({ [itemId]: quantity });
          } else {
            console.error(`Could not update ${itemId} to ${quantity}`);
          }
        }
      }
    },

    /**
     * Redirect to checkout
     */
    navigateToCheckout() {
      if (!this.isCartEmpty) {
        this.loading = true;
        window.location = `/checkout?locale=${app.currentLang}`;
      }
    },

    /**
     * Scroll the items list to the top
     */
    scrollItemsToTop() {
      const { itemsList } = this.$refs;

      if (itemsList) {
        jQuery(itemsList).animate({ scrollTop: 0 }, 300);
      }
    },

    /**
     * Update target element text to match cart total item count
     */
    updateCartItemCountEls() {
      const { item_count: count } = this.cart;
      const countEls = document.querySelectorAll('.cart-item-count');

      if (countEls) {
        countEls.forEach(el => {
          el.innerText = count;
        });
      }
    },

    removeSoldOutItems() {
      const [ lastAddedItem ] = this.cart.items
      const isSoldOutCheck = product => product.tags.split(', ').some(tag => tag === 'sold-out')

      const removeLastAddedItem = () => {
        CartJS.removeItemById(lastAddedItem.id)
      }

      if(lastAddedItem && lastAddedItem.handle) {
        fetch(`/products/${lastAddedItem.handle}.json`)
          .then(data => data.json())
          .then(({ product }) => isSoldOutCheck(product))
          .then(isSoldOut => isSoldOut && removeLastAddedItem())
      }
    },

    onCartOpen() {
      const { id, items } = this.cart

      // Track
      Segment.track('Cart Viewed', {
        cart_id: id,
        products: items.map((item, i) => ({
          product_id: item.product_id,
          sku: item.sku,
          category: item.product_type,
          name: item.product_title,
          brand: item.vendor,
          variant: item.variant_id,
          price: Segment.centsToMoney(item.price),
          quantity: item.quantity,
          coupon: '',
          position: i,
          url: `https://${window.location.host}${item.url}`,
          image_url: item.image,
        })),
      })

      // Disable body scrolling
      this.tmpScrollTop = jQuery(window).scrollTop()
      jQuery('body').css('overflow', 'hidden')

      // Reset the mobile mode to items
      this.setMobileMode(this.mobileModes.ITEMS)

      // Reset scroll
      this.scrollItemsToTop()
    },

    onCartClose() {
      // Enable body scrolling
      jQuery('body').css('overflow', 'auto')
      jQuery(window).scrollTop(this.tmpScrollTop)
    },

    onItemAdd(item, itemIndex) {
      // Track
      Segment.track('Product Added', {
        cart_id: '',
        product_id: item.product_id,
        sku: item.sku,
        category: item.product_type,
        name: item.product_title,
        brand: item.vendor,
        variant: item.variant_id,
        price: Segment.centsToMoney(item.price),
        quantity: item.quantity,
        coupon: '',
        position: itemIndex,
        url: `https://${window.location.host}${item.url}`,
        image_url: item.image,
      })
    },

    onItemRemove(item, itemIndex) {
      // Track
      Segment.track('Product Removed', {
        cart_id: '',
        product_id: item.product_id,
        sku: item.sku,
        category: item.product_type,
        name: item.product_title,
        brand: item.vendor,
        variant: item.variant_id,
        price: Segment.centsToMoney(item.price),
        quantity: item.quantity,
        coupon: '',
        position: itemIndex,
        url: `https://${window.location.host}${item.url}`,
        image_url: item.image,
      })
    },
  },

  watch: {
    /**
     * @param {Array} items
     * @param {Array} prevItems
     */
    cartItems(items, prevItems) {
      // Update counts
      this.updateCartItemCountEls()

      // Update quantity change check
      const totalQty = items
        .map(({ quantity }) => parseInt(quantity))
        .reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0)
      const prevTotalQty = prevItems
        .map(({ quantity }) => parseInt(quantity))
        .reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0)

      this.wasQuantityReduced = totalQty < prevTotalQty

      // On items change
      const addedItems = items.filter(
        (item) => !prevItems.map((x) => x.id).includes(item.id),
      )
      const removedItems = prevItems.filter(
        (item) => !items.map((x) => x.id).includes(item.id),
      )

      for (const item of addedItems) {
        const itemIndex = items.findIndex(({ id }) => id === item.id)

        this.onItemAdd(item, itemIndex)
      }

      for (const item of removedItems) {
        const itemIndex = prevItems.findIndex(({ id }) => id === item.id)

        this.onItemRemove(item, itemIndex)
      }

      if (addedItems.length) {
        // Scroll items to top if added
        this.scrollItemsToTop()

        // Remove item if it has "sold-out" tag
        this.removeSoldOutItems()
      }

      // Check cart product links and limits
      this.checkCartProductQuantities()
    },

    /**
     * @param {boolean} state
     */
    open(state) {
      if (state) {
        this.onCartOpen()
      } else {
        this.onCartClose()
      }
    },

    /**
     * @param {Array} variants
     */
    suggestedVariants(variants) {
      if (!variants.length) {
        // Switch to items mode when no suggested items remain
        this.setMobileMode(this.mobileModes.ITEMS);
      }
    },
  },

  mounted() {
    // Body ready actions
    jQuery(() => {
      this.updateCartItemCountEls();
    });

    // Cart events
    jQuery(document).on('cart.requestStarted', this.onBeforeCartUpdate);
    jQuery(document).on('cart.requestComplete', this.onCartUpdate);
  },

  beforeDestroy() {
    jQuery(document).off('cart.requestStarted', this.onBeforeCartUpdate);
    jQuery(document).off('cart.requestComplete', this.onCartUpdate);
  },
});
</script>

  <script type="text/x-template" id="cart-banner">
  <transition name="slide-fade" :duration="transitionDuration" v-on:after-enter="setPageContainerPadding" v-on:after-leave="setPageContainerPadding">
    <div class="cartBanner" v-show="canShow">
      <div class="cartBanner__outer">
        <div class="cartBanner__inner">
          <div class="shipping-info">
            <span class="icon icon-box"></span>
            <div v-html="$t('general.free_shipping')"></div>
          </div>
          <div class="cartBanner__items flexslider carousel" ref="itemsList">
            <ul class="slides" ref="itemsListSlides">
              <li v-for="item in cart.items">
                <cart-product-item
                  :id="item.id"
                  :title="item.title"
                  :image="item.image"
                  :price="item.final_price"
                  :quantity="item.quantity"
                  :disabled="loading"
                  :url="item.url"
                  :hide-details="true"
                ></cart-product-item>
              </li>
            </ul>
          </div>
          <div class="totals-info">
            <span class="nowrap">${ $t('cart.total_price') }:</span>
            <strong v-html="Shopify.formatMoney(cart.total_price)"></strong>
            <div class="small light nowrap" v-html="Shopify.formatMoney(cart.total_price, false, true) + ' ' + $t('general.vat_incl')"></div>
          </div>
          <button class="btn btn--cart" @click="$root.openCart">${ $t('cart.view_cart') }</button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  </transition>
</script>

<script>
Vue.component('cart-banner', {
  template: '#cart-banner',

  props: {
    show: Boolean,
  },

  delimiters: ['${', '}'],

  data() {
    return {
      loading: false,
      cart: CartJS.cart,
      delayedShow: this.show,
      Shopify,
    }
  },

  computed: {
    /**
     * Disable transition animation on small devices
     *
     * @returns {number}
     */
    transitionDuration() {
      const { isMobileResolution, isTabletResolution } = this.$root

      return isMobileResolution || isTabletResolution ? 0 : 300
    },

    /**
     * Check if the banner can be shown
     *
     * @returns {boolean}
     */
    canShow() {
      return this.delayedShow && !this.isCartEmpty
    },

    /**
     * Cart items shortcut, always returns an array
     *
     * @returns {Array}
     */
    cartItems() {
      return this.cart.items || []
    },

    /**
     * Check if there are items in the cart
     *
     * @returns {boolean}
     */
    isCartEmpty() {
      return this.cartItems.length === 0
    },
  },

  methods: {
    /**
     * Send a custom close event for the parent to handle
     */
    closeBanner() {
      this.$emit('close')
    },

    /**
     * Enable loading when the cart is about to update
     */
    onBeforeCartUpdate() {
      this.loading = true
    },

    /**
     * Update component data on cart update
     *
     * @param {Object} event
     * @param {Object} cart
     */
    onCartUpdate(event, cart) {
      this.cart = cart
      this.loading = false
    },

    /**
     * Additional page container padding for the banner to not overlap content
     */
    setPageContainerPadding() {
      const containerEl = document.getElementById('PageContainer')

      if (containerEl) {
        containerEl.style.paddingBottom = this.canShow
          ? `${this.$el.offsetHeight}px`
          : 0
      }
    },

    /**
     * Scroll the items list to the left
     */
    scrollItemsToLeft() {
      const { itemsListSlides } = this.$refs

      if (itemsListSlides) {
        jQuery(itemsListSlides).css('transform', 'translate3d(0, 0, 0)')
      }
    },

    /**
     * Create or reset the banner items flexslider
     */
    itemsSlider() {
      const { itemsList } = this.$refs

      if (typeof jQuery.flexslider === 'function') {
        const flexsliderData = jQuery(itemsList).data('flexslider')

        if (!flexsliderData) {
          // Initialize slider
          jQuery(itemsList).flexslider({
            animation: 'slide',
            animationLoop: false,
            controlNav: false,
            itemWidth: 100,
            itemMargin: 10,
            slideshow: false,
          })
        } else {
          // Reset the settings
          flexsliderData.setup()
        }
      }
    },
  },

  watch: {
    /**
     * @param {Array} items
     * @param {Array} prevItems
     */
    cartItems(items, prevItems) {
      const hasNewItems = items.some((item) => !prevItems.includes(item))

      this.$nextTick(() => {
        // Always reset the slider
        this.itemsSlider()

        if (hasNewItems) {
          this.scrollItemsToLeft()
        }
      })
    },

    /**
     * @param {Boolean} state
     */
    show(state) {
      setTimeout(() => {
        this.delayedShow = state
        // Reset slider
        this.itemsSlider()
      }, 200)
    },
  },

  mounted() {
    jQuery(() => {
      this.setPageContainerPadding()
      this.itemsSlider()

      // Trigger resize to re-init slider (weird bug)
      jQuery(window).trigger('resize')
    })
    jQuery(window).on('resize', () => {
      this.setPageContainerPadding()
      this.$nextTick(this.itemsSlider)
    })
    jQuery(document).on('scroll', this.setPageContainerPadding)
    jQuery(document).on('cart.requestStarted', this.onBeforeCartUpdate)
    jQuery(document).on('cart.requestComplete', this.onCartUpdate)
  },
})
</script>
  <script type="text/x-template" id="cart-product-item">
  <div class="cart-product-item">
    <div class="item-image">
      <template v-if="url">
        <a :href="url">
          <img :src="image">
        </a>
      </template>
      <template v-else>
        <img :src="image">
      </template>
      <div class="item-image-price" v-show="hideDetails" v-html="$root.formatMoney(finalPrice)"></div>
    </div>
    <div class="item-details" v-show="!hideDetails">
      <div class="item-title">
        <template v-if="url">
          <a :href="url">
            ${title}
          </a>
        </template>
        <template v-else>
          ${title}
        </template>
      </div>
      <div class="item-price" v-html="$root.formatMoney(finalPrice)"></div>
      <slot></slot>
    </div>
    <div class="item-qty-controls" :class="{ 'disabled': disabled }">
      <template v-if="quantity === 0">
        <div class="qty-control qty-cart" @click="increaseQty">
          <img class="icon icon-cart" :src="$root.asset('icon-add-to-cart.svg')">
        </div>
      </template>
      <template v-else>
        <div
          class="qty-control qty-plus"
          :class="{ 'disabled': !canIncreaseQty }"
          @click="increaseQty"
        >
          &plus;
        </div>
        <div class="qty-control qty-amount">
          <input
            maxlength="4"
            :value="quantity"
            @blur="updateQtyFromInput"
            @keyup.enter="updateQtyFromInput"
          >
        </div>
        <div
          class="qty-control qty-minus"
          :class="{ 'disabled': !canDecreaseQty }"
          @click="decreaseQty"
        >
          &ndash;
        </div>
      </template>
    </div>
  </div>
</script>

<script>
Vue.component('cart-product-item', {
  template: '#cart-product-item',

  props: {
    id: Number,
    title: String,
    image: String,
    price: Number,
    quantity: Number,
    disabled: Boolean,
    url: String,
    hideDetails: Boolean,
  },

  data() {
    return {
      limit: {},
      isLimitEnabled: false,
    };
  },

  delimiters: ['${', '}'],

  computed: {
    /**
     * Base price multiplied by the quantity
     * Shows the base price for both 0 and 1 quantities
     *
     * @returns {number}
     */
    finalPrice() {
      return this.quantity > 0 ? this.price * this.quantity : this.price;
    },

    /**
     * Get the item product ID
     *
     * @returns {number}
     */
    productId() {
      const item = CartJS.cart.items.find(item => item.id === this.id);

      return item && parseInt(item.product_id);
    },

    /**
     * Check if the quantity can be increased
     *
     * @returns {boolean}
     */
    canIncreaseQty() {
      if (this.localQuantity >= 9999) {
        return false;
      };

      if (!this.isLimitEnabled) {
        return true;
      };

      return this.localQuantity < this.limit.max;
    },

    /**
     * Check if the quantity can be decreased
     *
     * @returns {boolean}
     */
    canDecreaseQty() {
      return this.localQuantity > 0
    },
  },

  methods: {
    /**
     * Update the product limits data
     */
    async setLimit () {
      const limits = await this.$root.getCustomerProductLimits()
      const limit = limits.some(limit => limit.variantId === this.id)

      if (limit) {
        this.limit = limit
        this.isLimitEnabled = true
      }
    },

    /**
     * Update cart item quantity
     *
     * @param {number} itemId
     * @param {number} quantity
     */
    updateQuantity(id, quantity) {
      if (!this.disabled) {
        CartJS.updateItemQuantitiesById({ [id]: quantity });
      }
    },

    /**
     * Helper method to increase cart item quantity
     */
    increaseQty() {
      this.canIncreaseQty && this.updateQuantity(this.id, this.quantity + 1);
    },

    /**
     * Helper method to decrease cart item quantity
     */
    decreaseQty() {
      this.updateQuantity(this.id, this.quantity - 1);
    },

    /**
     * Update quantity from input value
     *
     * @param {Event} event
     */
    updateQtyFromInput(event) {
      const { value } = event.target;
      const newQuantity = parseInt(value);

      if (newQuantity >= 0) {
        // Update the value if it's changed
        if (newQuantity !== this.quantity) {
          this.updateQuantity(this.id, newQuantity);
        }
      } else {
        // Reset the initial quantity
        event.target.value = this.quantity;
      }
    },
  },

  created() {
    this.setLimit()
  },
});
</script>

var LySwitcherDrawer = LySwitcherDrawer || {
  templateList: new Array(),
  init: function() {
    LySwitcherDrawer._fetchDrawerData();
    setTimeout(function() {
      for(var i=0; i<LySwitcherDrawer.templateList.length; i++) {
        var template = LySwitcherDrawer.templateList[i];

        if(template.target){
          var $orientationTargets = $('body').find(template.target);
        } else {
          var $orientationTargets = $('body').find('a[href="/cart"], a[href="#cart"], .cart-toggle, .site-header__cart');
        }

        $orientationTargets.each(function() {
          LySwitcherDrawer._draw(template, $(this));
        });
      }
      LySwitcherDrawer._bindSwitcherEvents();
    }, 500);
  },
  _fetchDrawerData: function() {
    var me = this;
    $('.ly-drawer-template').each(function(i) {
      me.templateList.push({
        id: i,
        align: $(this).data('align'),
        target: $(this).data('target'),
        targetIsContainer: $(this).data('target-is-container'),
        type: $(this).data('type'),
        css: $(this).data('css'),
        class: $(this).data('class'),
        template: $(this).html()
      });
      $(this).remove();
    });
  },


  _draw: function(template, $orientationTarget) {
    var $switcherElem = null;
    var switcherHtml = template.template;
    var $target = $orientationTarget;
    if(template.targetIsContainer === true) {
      if(template.align === 'left') {
        $switcherElem = $orientationTarget.prepend(switcherHtml);
      } else if(template.align === 'right') {
        $switcherElem = $orientationTarget.append(switcherHtml);
      } else {
        $switcherElem = $orientationTarget.append(switcherHtml);
      }
    } else {
      if(template.align === 'left') {
        $switcherElem = $orientationTarget.before(switcherHtml);
      } else if(template.align === 'right') {
        $switcherElem = $orientationTarget.after(switcherHtml);
      } else {
        $switcherElem = $orientationTarget.after(switcherHtml);
      }
    }
    $switcherElem.find('.ly-languages-switcher-dropdown, .ly-languages-image-dropdown-switcher, .ly-languages-image-dropdown-icons-switcher, .ly-languages-links-switcher, .ly-languages-links-icons-switcher').attr('style', template.css);
  },
  _bindSwitcherEvents: function() {
    $('.ly-languages-image-dropdown-switcher, .ly-languages-image-dropdown-icons-switcher').click(function(e) {
      e.preventDefault();
      var dropdownList = $(this).find('ul');
      if($(this).data('dropup') === true) {
        dropdownList.css('bottom', $(this).outerHeight());
      } else {
        dropdownList.css('top', $(this).outerHeight());
      }
      if($(this).hasClass('ly-is-open')) {
        $(this).removeClass('ly-is-open');
        dropdownList.attr('style', 'display:none !important;')
      } else {
        $(this).addClass('ly-is-open');
        if($(this).data('dropup') === true) {
          dropdownList.attr('style', 'display:inline-block !important;bottom:' + $(this).outerHeight() + 'px')
        } else {
          dropdownList.attr('style', 'display:inline-block !important;top:' + $(this).outerHeight() + 'px')
        }
      }
    });
    $('.ly-languages-link').click(function (e) {
      langify.helper.saveLanguage(this.id);
    });
    $('.ly-languages-switcher-dropdown').change(function(e) {
      langify.helper.saveLanguage($(this).val());
    });
  },
};

                  },
                },
                financial_status: {
                  voided: 'キャンセル済み',
                  pending: '処理中',
                  authorized: '認証済み',
                  refunded: '返金済み',
                  paid: '支払済み',
                },
                fulfillment_status: {
                  fulfilled: '発送済',
                  unfulfilled: '未発送',
                  partially_fulfilled: '',
                },
              },
            },
          };
        },

        computed: {
          t() {
            return this.translations[this.currentLang] ?? this.translations['en']
          },
        },

        methods: {
          /**
           * Return unique array values
           *
           * @returns {Array}
           */
           onlyUnique(value, index, self) {
            return self.indexOf(value) === index;
          },

          /**
           * Used to get translations that have a variable placeholder
           */
          tArg(translationKey, value, ndValue) {
            const variablePlaceholder = '{n}'
            const ndVariablePlaceholder = '{k}'

            const translationKeys = translationKey.split('.')
            let result = this.t;

            for (const key of translationKeys) {
              result = result[key]
            }

            if (!result || typeof result !== 'string') {
              console.error('Cannot find translation for: ', translationKey)
              return ''
            }

            if (!result.includes(variablePlaceholder)) {
              console.error('Translation string does not have variable slot: ', translationKey)
              return ''
            }

            const first = result.replace(variablePlaceholder, value)

            if (ndValue) {
              return first.replace(ndVariablePlaceholder, ndValue)
            }

            return first;
          },

          /**
           * @returns {Object[]}
           */
          getBoughtItemQtiesGroupedBySku() {
            const boughtItems = this.appData.boughtItems;
            const boughtItemQties = {};

            for (const { sku, qty } of boughtItems) {
              const oldQty = boughtItemQties[sku] || 0;

              boughtItemQties[sku] = oldQty + qty;
            }

            return boughtItemQties;
          },

          /**
           * Group GET request parameters as an object
           *
           * @returns {Object}
           */
          searchParams() {
            const paramsMap = window.location.search
              .replace('?', '')
              .split('&')
              .map(param => param.split('='));

            // Convert the params map to an object
            const params = {};

            for (const [key, value] of paramsMap) {
              params[key] = value;
            }

            return params;
          },

          /**
           * Set resolution booleans
           */
          checkResolutions() {
            const ww = window.outerWidth;

            this.isMobileResolution = ww <= this.breakpoints.MOBILE;
            this.isTabletResolution = ww <= this.breakpoints.TABLET;
          },

          /**
           * Helper method to fetch asset with typecheck
           */
          asset(key, fallback = null) {
            const asset = this.appData.assets[key];

            return typeof asset !== 'undefined' ? asset : fallback;
          },

          /**
           * Helper method to fetch asset with typecheck
           */
          // t(key, context, fallback = null) {
          //   console.log(this.translations);
          //   console.log(this.activeLanguage);
          //   // return context.translations[this.activeLanguage][key]
          // },

          /**
           * Open the cart modal
           */
          openCart() {
            this.isCartModalOpen = true;
          },

          /**
           * Close the cart modal
           */
          closeCart() {
            this.isCartModalOpen = false;
          },

          /**
           * Show the cart banner
           */
          showCartBanner() {
            this.isCartBannerShown = true;
          },

          /**
           * Hide the cart banner
           */
          hideCartBanner() {
            this.isCartBannerShown = false;
          },

          /**
           * Helper method to format money
           *
           * @param {number} cents
           * @returns {string}
           */
          formatMoney(cents, applyVat = false) {
            const money = this.Shopify.formatMoney(cents, false, applyVat);
            return `<span class="nowrap">${money}</span>`;
          },

          formatMoneySimple(cents, applyVat = false) {
            const money = this.Shopify.formatMoney(cents, false, applyVat);
            return `${money}`;
          },

          /**
           * Set-up all cart related actions
           */
          initCart() {
            // Initiate CartJS
            CartJS.init(this.appData.cart, {
              'requestBodyClass': 'loading',
              'moneyFormat': '¥ {{amount}}',
              'moneyWithCurrencyFormat': '¥ {{amount}}'
            });

            // Open the cart if requested
            if (window.location.search === "?cart") {
              window.history.replaceState({}, null, window.location.pathname);
              this.openCart();
            }

            // Handle cart header menu item
            jQuery(document).on('click', '.site-header__cart-toggle', e => {
              e.preventDefault();
              this.openCart();
            });
          },

          setProductSku() {
            // console.log();

            const { product } = this.appData;
            const { variant: variantId } = this.searchParams();
            const skuEl = document.querySelector('.product-current-sku');

            if (product && skuEl) {
              // Use the first variant by default
              let variant = product.variants[0];

              if (variantId) {
                // Find the variant based on the request parameter
                variant = product.variants.find(
                  variant => parseInt(variant.id) === parseInt(variantId)
                );
              }

              if (variant) {
                // Update the element text
                skuEl.innerText = variant.sku;
              }
            }
          },

          makeSlug(text) {
            return text.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]+/g, '-').replace(/-$/, '').replace(/^-/, '');
          },

          getUrlParameter(sParam) {
              var sPageURL = decodeURIComponent(window.location.search.substring(1)),
              sURLVariables = sPageURL.split('&'),
              sParameterName,
              i;

              for (i = 0; i < sURLVariables.length; i++) {
              sParameterName = sURLVariables[i].split('=');

              if (sParameterName[0] === sParam) {
                  return sParameterName[1] === undefined ? true : sParameterName[1];
              }
              }
          },

          replaceUrlParam(e,r,a){
            var n=new RegExp("("+r+"=).*?(&|$)"),c=e;return c=e.search(n)>=0?e.replace(n,"$1"+a+"$2"):c+(c.indexOf("?")>0?"&":"?")+r+"="+a
          },

          /**
           * Handle [data-toggle] that toggles [data-toggle-id] elements
           */
          handleDataToggle(e) {
            const $action = jQuery(e.currentTarget);
            const targetId = $action.data('toggle');
            const $target = jQuery(`[data-toggle-id="${targetId}"]`);

            const toggleText = $action.attr('data-toggle-text');
            const toggleTextNew = $action.attr('data-toggle-text-new');
            const toggleTextTarget = $action.children('[data-toggle-text-target]').first();

            const forceOpen = typeof $action.data('toggle-open') !== 'undefined';
            const forceClose = typeof $action.data('toggle-close') !== 'undefined' && !forceOpen;

            e.preventDefault();

            if ($action.hasClass('active') || forceClose) {
              if (!forceOpen) {
                $target.removeClass('active');
                $target.stop(true).slideUp(300);
                $action.removeClass('active');
              }
            } else if (!$action.hasClass('active') || forceOpen) {
              if (!forceClose) {
                $target.addClass('active');
                $target.stop(true).slideDown(300);
                $action.addClass('active');
              }
            }

            if(!!toggleText && !!toggleTextNew && !!toggleTextTarget) {
              $action.hasClass('active') ? toggleTextTarget.text(toggleTextNew) : toggleTextTarget.text(toggleText);
            }

          },

          /**
           * Handle [data-scroll-to] that scrolls to [data-scroll-to-id] elements
           */
          handleDataScrollTo(e) {
            const $action = jQuery(e.currentTarget);
            const targetId = $action.data('scroll-to');
            const $target = jQuery(`[data-scroll-to-id="${targetId}"]`);

            jQuery('html, body').animate({
              scrollTop: $target.offset().top,
            }, 600);
          },

          /**
           * Fetch and parse a cart attribute
           *
           * @param {string} name
           * @returns {Object}
           */
          getCartAttribute(name) {
            const attributes = CartJS.getAttributes();
            const attribute = attributes && attributes[name] ? attributes[name] : '{}';

            return JSON.parse(attribute.replace(/=>/g, ':'));
          },

          /**
           * @param {boolean} forceUpdate
           * @returns {Promise<{ sku: string; max: string }[]>}
           */
          async getCustomerProductLimits(forceUpdate = false) {
            if (!this.customerProductLimits || forceUpdate) {
              const response = await fetch('/apps/shop-manager/api/product-limits', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: {
                  Accept: 'application/json',
                  'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                },
                body: JSON.stringify({ shop: Shopify.shop }),
              })

              if (!response.ok) {
                this.customerProductLimits = [];
              } else {
                this.customerProductLimits = await response.json();
              }
            }

            return this.customerProductLimits;
          },

          /**
           * Handle login referral redirect
           *
           * @returns {void}
           */
          handleLoginReferral() {
            if (!localStorage) {
              return
            }

            // If referral exists and not on login page
            const accountLoginRef = localStorage.getItem('account-login-ref')
            const isLoginPage = location.pathname === '/account/login'

            if (!accountLoginRef || isLoginPage) {
              return
            }

            // Remove the item
            localStorage.removeItem('account-login-ref')

            // Only if on account page (after login)
            const isAccountPage = location.pathname === '/account'

            if (!isAccountPage) {
              return
            }

            // Redirect to the referred url
            window.location = accountLoginRef
          },
          redirectToLogin() {
            // Set a local storage referral url to current page
            if (localStorage) {
              localStorage.setItem('account-login-ref', location.href)
            }

            // Redirect
            location.href = '/account/login';
          },
          },

        created() {
          this.checkResolutions();
          this.initCart();
        },

        mounted() {
          this.setProductSku();
          this.handleLoginReferral()

          // Events
          jQuery(window).on('resize', this.checkResolutions);
          jQuery(document).on('click', '[data-toggle]', this.handleDataToggle);
          jQuery(document).on('click', '[data-scroll-to]', this.handleDataScrollTo);

          // pushState event hack
          const pushState = history.pushState;
          history.pushState = (...args) => {
            pushState.apply(history, args);

            // Custom events
            this.setProductSku();
          };
        },
      });
    </script>


  

  
  <script type="text/x-template" id="checkbox">
  <button
    type="button"
    class="custom-checkbox relative"
    :class="getClasses()"
    :disabled="disabled"
    @click="(e) => $emit('click', e)"
  >
    <svg class="custom-checkbox__check" width="8" height="6" viewBox="0 0 8 6" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M2.93801 4.57502L1.17056 2.80756C0.975298 2.61231 0.65872 2.61231 0.463461 2.80756C0.268239 3.00279 0.268196 3.31929 0.463365 3.51456L1.94798 4.99999L2.00002 5.05003L2.2319 5.28191C2.62242 5.67243 3.25559 5.67243 3.64611 5.28191L7.53548 1.39254C7.73073 1.19729 7.73073 0.88074 7.53548 0.685496C7.34025 0.490268 7.02373 0.490249 6.82848 0.685454L2.93801 4.57502Z" fill="white"/></svg>
    <div class="custom-checkbox__line"></div>
  </button>

<script data-ot-ignore type="text/javascript">
  Vue.component('checkbox', {
    props: {
      checked: {
        type: Boolean,
        default: false,
      },
      disabled: {
        type: Boolean,
        default: false,
      },
      classes: {
        type: String,
        default: '',
      },
    },
    methods: {
      getClasses() {
        if (this.checked) {
          return `${this.classes} checked`
        }
        return this.classes
      }
    },
    template: '#checkbox',
    delimiters: ['${', '}'],
  });
</script>

<style>
  .custom-checkbox {
    width: 16px;
    min-width: 16px;
    height: 16px;
    min-height: 16px;
    background: #fff;
    border-radius: 4px;
    border: 1px solid #B6B9C4;
  }
  /* Disabled state */
  .custom-checkbox:disabled {
    border: 1px solid #DBDCE1;
  }
  /* Checked state */
  .custom-checkbox.checked {
    border: 1px solid #006FFF;
    background: #006FFF;
  }
  /* Disabled state & Checked state */
  .checked.custom-checkbox:disabled {
    border: 1px solid #CCE2FF;
    background: #CCE2FF;
  }
  /* Svg for disabled but not checked state */
  .custom-checkbox__line {
    visibility: hidden;
    position: absolute;
    top: 50%;
    left: 50%;
    transform: translate(-50%, -50%);
    width: 50%;
    height: 1px;
    background: #838691;
  }
  .custom-checkbox:disabled .custom-checkbox__line {
    visibility: visible;
  }
  .checked .custom-checkbox__line {
    visibility: hidden !important;
  }
  /* Svg for checked state */
  .custom-checkbox__check {
    visibility: hidden;
    position: absolute;
    top: 50%;
    left: 50%;
    transform: translate(-50%, -50%);
  }
  .checked .custom-checkbox__check {
    visibility: visible;
  }
</style>

<script type="text/x-template" id="product-bisn">
  <div class="bisn add8top one-whole">
    <template v-if="isLoggedIn">
      <div class="flex bisn-checkbox-wrapper">
        <checkbox
          :checked="subscribed"
          :disabled="loading"
          @click="onCheckboxChange"
        ></checkbox>
        <span class="add8left bisn-checkbox-text" style="font-size: 14px; line-heigth: 24px; color: rgba(0,0,0,.65);">再入荷した際にメールで教えてください</span>
      </div>
      <div v-if="!hideAdditionalText" class="add24left" style="line-height: 20px; font-size: 12px; color: rgba(0,0,0,.45);">
        Restock notifications are sent to customers in the order they are requested.
        If you don't get an email, it's likely because we only received enough product for those that requested notification before you.
        <!-- <a href="https://br.store.ui.com/a/faq#NOTIFICAESDEESTOQUE">こちら</a> -->
      </div>
    </template>
    <div style="color: #0E0E0E; font-size: 14px;" v-else>
      ${t.product.bisn} <a style="padding: 4px 8px; line-height: 14.4px; font-size: 12px; margin-bottom: 2px;" class="btn btn--small add8left" @click="$root.redirectToLogin">ログイン</a>
    </div>
  </div>
</script>

<script data-ot-ignore type="text/javascript">
Vue.component('product-bisn', {
  template: '#product-bisn',

  delimiters: ['${', '}'],

  props: {
    customerId: [Number, String],
    email: String,
    productId: [Number, String],
    sku: String,
    hideAdditionalText: {
      type: Boolean,
      default: false,
    },
  },

  data() {
    return {
      t: app.t,
      apiUrl: '/apps/shop-manager/api',
      subscribed: false,
      loading: false,
    }
  },

  computed: {
    isLoggedIn() {
      return this.customerId > 0
    },
  },

  methods: {
    getRequestData() {
      const { shop } = Shopify
      const { customerId, email, productId, sku } = this.$props

      return {
        shop,
        customerId: `${customerId}`,
        email,
        productId: `${productId}`,
        sku,
        subscribe: this.subscribed,
      }
    },

    async sendPostRequest(url, data) {
      const rawResponse = await fetch(url, {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: {
          'Accept': 'application/json',
          'Content-Type': 'application/json',
        },
        body: JSON.stringify(data),
      })

      return rawResponse.status === 200 && rawResponse.json()
    },

    async checkIfSubscribed() {
      this.loading = true

      const result = await this.sendPostRequest(
        `${this.apiUrl}/bisn/subscribed`,
        this.getRequestData(),
      )

      this.subscribed = !!result
      this.loading = false
    },

    async onCheckboxChange() {
      this.loading = true

      // Update state
      this.subscribed = !this.subscribed

      // Update subscription
      try {
        const result = await this.sendPostRequest(
          `${this.apiUrl}/bisn`,
          this.getRequestData(),
        )

        if (!result) throw new Error()
      } catch (e) {
        // Revert state
        this.subscribed = !this.subscribed
      }

      this.loading = false
    },
  },

  created() {
    this.checkIfSubscribed()
  },
})
</script>

var translateTextNode = function(node) {
if(node.textContent && node.textContent.trim().length > 0) {
var src = node.textContent.trim().replace(/(\r\n|\n|\r)/gm,"").replace(/\s+/g," ").toUpperCase();
if(customContents[src] && node.textContent !== customContents[src]) {
var newContent = node.textContent.replace(node.textContent.trim(), customContents[src]); if (newContent != node.textContent) { node.textContent = newContent }
}
}
}
try {var textNodes = $('body').find('*').addBack().not('script').not('style').contents().filter(function() {
if(this.nodeType === 3) {
translateTextNode(this);
}
});
} catch(e) {};var target = document.querySelector('body');

mutations.forEach(function(mutation) {
var newNodes = mutation.addedNodes;
if(newNodes) {
for(i = 0; i < newNodes.length; i++) {
try {var textNodes = $(newNodes[i]).find('*').addBack().not('script').not('style').contents().filter(function() {
if(this.nodeType === 3) {
translateTextNode(this);
}
});
} catch(e) {};}
}
if(mutation.type === 'characterData') {
translateTextNode(mutation.target);
}
});
});
var config = { childList: true, characterData: true, subtree: true }
observer.observe(target, config);

  init: function() {

    setTimeout(function() {
      for(var i=0; i<LySwitcherDrawer.templateList.length; i++) {
        var template = LySwitcherDrawer.templateList[i];

        if(template.target){
          var $orientationTargets = $('body').find(template.target);
        } else {
          var $orientationTargets = $('body').find('a[href="/cart"], a[href="#cart"], .cart-toggle, .site-header__cart');
        }

        $orientationTargets.each(function() {
          LySwitcherDrawer._draw(template, $(this));
        });
      }
      LySwitcherDrawer._bindSwitcherEvents();
    }, 500);
  },
  _fetchDrawerData: function() {
    var me = this;
    $('.ly-drawer-template').each(function(i) {
      me.templateList.push({
        id: i,
        align: $(this).data('align'),
        target: $(this).data('target'),
        targetIsContainer: $(this).data('target-is-container'),
        type: $(this).data('type'),
        css: $(this).data('css'),
        class: $(this).data('class'),
        template: $(this).html()
      });
      $(this).remove();
    });
  },


  _draw: function(template, $orientationTarget) {
    var $switcherElem = null;
    var switcherHtml = template.template;
    var $target = $orientationTarget;
    if(template.targetIsContainer === true) {
      if(template.align === 'left') {
        $switcherElem = $orientationTarget.prepend(switcherHtml);
      } else if(template.align === 'right') {
        $switcherElem = $orientationTarget.append(switcherHtml);
      } else {
        $switcherElem = $orientationTarget.append(switcherHtml);
      }
    } else {
      if(template.align === 'left') {
        $switcherElem = $orientationTarget.before(switcherHtml);
      } else if(template.align === 'right') {
        $switcherElem = $orientationTarget.after(switcherHtml);
      } else {
        $switcherElem = $orientationTarget.after(switcherHtml);
      }
    }
    $switcherElem.find('.ly-languages-switcher-dropdown, .ly-languages-image-dropdown-switcher, .ly-languages-image-dropdown-icons-switcher, .ly-languages-links-switcher, .ly-languages-links-icons-switcher').attr('style', template.css);
  },
  _bindSwitcherEvents: function() {
    $('.ly-languages-image-dropdown-switcher, .ly-languages-image-dropdown-icons-switcher').click(function(e) {
      e.preventDefault();
      var dropdownList = $(this).find('ul');
      if($(this).data('dropup') === true) {
        dropdownList.css('bottom', $(this).outerHeight());
      } else {
        dropdownList.css('top', $(this).outerHeight());
      }
      if($(this).hasClass('ly-is-open')) {
        $(this).removeClass('ly-is-open');
        dropdownList.attr('style', 'display:none !important;')
      } else {
        $(this).addClass('ly-is-open');
        if($(this).data('dropup') === true) {
          dropdownList.attr('style', 'display:inline-block !important;bottom:' + $(this).outerHeight() + 'px')
        } else {
          dropdownList.attr('style', 'display:inline-block !important;top:' + $(this).outerHeight() + 'px')
        }
      }
    });
    $('.ly-languages-link').click(function (e) {
      langify.helper.saveLanguage(this.id);
    });
    $('.ly-languages-switcher-dropdown').change(function(e) {
      langify.helper.saveLanguage($(this).val());
    });
  },
};

          ${currency.code} (${currency.name})
        </option>
      </select>

      <p class="notice">*All payments can proceed only in EUR<br />(Euro) currency</p>
    </template>

    <button class="btn btn--full" @click="openShop">Browse ${shop.name}</button>
  </template>
</div>

<script data-ot-ignore type="text/javascript">

new Vue({
  el: '#geoSelectApp',

  delimiters: ['${', '}'],

  data() {
    return {
      currentShopOrigin: Shopify.shop,
      geoCountry: null,
      shop: null,
      selectedCountryCode: null,
      selectedCurrencyCode: CURRENCY.EUR.code,
      shops: [
        {
          origin: 'truff.myshopify.com',
          url: 'https://store.ui.com',
          name: 'USA Store',
          countries: [COUNTRY.US],
        },
        {
          origin: 'store-ui-canada.myshopify.com',
          url: 'https://ca.store.ui.com',
          name: 'Canada Store',
          countries: [COUNTRY.CA],
        },
        {
          origin: 'store-ui-japan.myshopify.com',
          url: 'https://jp.store.ui.com',
          name: 'Japan Store',
          countries: [COUNTRY.JP],
        },
        {
          origin: 'store-ui-mexico.myshopify.com',
          url: 'https://mx.store.ui.com',
          name: 'Mexico Store',
          countries: [COUNTRY.MX],
        },
        {
          origin: 'store-ui-india.myshopify.com',
          url: 'https://in.store.ui.com',
          name: 'India Store',
          countries: [COUNTRY.IN],
        },
        {
          origin: 'store-ui-taiwan.myshopify.com',
          url: 'https://tw.store.ui.com',
          name: 'Taiwan Store',
          countries: [COUNTRY.TW],
        },
        {
          origin: 'store-ui-europe.myshopify.com',
          url: 'https://eu.store.ui.com',
          name: 'Europe Store',
          countries: [
            COUNTRY.AT,
            COUNTRY.BE,
            COUNTRY.BG,
            COUNTRY.HR,
            COUNTRY.CZ,
            COUNTRY.DK,
            COUNTRY.EE,
            COUNTRY.FI,
            COUNTRY.FR,
            COUNTRY.DE,
            COUNTRY.EL,
            COUNTRY.ES,
            COUNTRY.HU,
            COUNTRY.IE,
            COUNTRY.IT,
            COUNTRY.LV,
            COUNTRY.LT,
            COUNTRY.LU,
            COUNTRY.NL,
            COUNTRY.PL,
            COUNTRY.PT,
            COUNTRY.RO,
            COUNTRY.SK,
            COUNTRY.SI,
            COUNTRY.SE,
            COUNTRY.CH,
            COUNTRY.UK,
          ],
        },
        {
          origin: "me.store.ui.com",
          url: "https://me.store.ui.com",
          name: "Middle East Store",
          countries: [COUNTRY.AE],
        },
      ],
      cookieKey: 'geo-select',
      canShow: false,
    }
  },

  computed: {
    hasCurrencySelect() {
      const shopOrigins = ['store-ui-europe.myshopify.com']

      return this.shop !== null && shopOrigins.includes(this.shop.origin)
    },

    currencySelectCurrencies() {
      const result = []

      if (this.hasCurrencySelect) {
        for (const { currency } of this.shop.countries) {
          if (!result.includes(currency)) {
            result.push(currency)
          }
        }
      }

      return result
    },
  },

  methods: {
    hasCookie() {
      return typeof jQuery.cookie(this.cookieKey) !== 'undefined'
    },

    setCookie(closeAction = false) {
      jQuery.cookie(this.cookieKey, closeAction ? '0' : '1', {
        expires: 30,
        path: '/',
      })
    },

    close() {
      // Set the cookie
      this.setCookie()

      // Hide the modal
      this.canShow = false
    },

    openShop() {
      if (!this.shop) {
        return
      }

      // Set the cookie
      this.setCookie()

      // Redirect
      const shopUrlParams = this.hasCurrencySelect
        ? '?' +
          [
            `refCountry=${this.selectedCountryCode}`,
            `refCurrency=${this.selectedCurrencyCode}`,
          ].join('&')
        : ''

      window.location = `${this.shop.url}${shopUrlParams}`
    },

    async initGeoCountry() {
      if (this.geoCountry) {
        return
      }

      try {
        const url = 'https://www.ui.com/api/geoip'
        const res = await fetch(url, { method: 'POST' })
        const { country_code: code, country_name: name } = await res.json()

        // Set the country as the selected country
        this.selectedCountryCode = code
        this.geoCountry = { code, name }
      } catch (e) {
          console.error('Failed to get country. ', e)
      }
    },

    initShop() {
      if (this.shop || !this.geoCountry) {
        return
      }

      for (const shop of this.shops) {
        const hasCountry = shop.countries.some(
          ({ code }) => code === this.geoCountry.code,
        )

        if (hasCountry) {
          this.shop = shop
          break
        }
      }
    },

    handleRefParams() {
      const { origin, searchParams } = new URL(location.href)
      let reloadPage = false

      // Set country
      const refCountry = searchParams.get('refCountry')

      if (refCountry) {
        jQuery.cookie('site-country', refCountry, {
          path: '/',
        })
        reloadPage = true
      }

      // Set currency
      const refCurrency = searchParams.get('refCurrency')

      if (refCurrency) {
        jQuery.cookie('site-currency', refCurrency, {
          path: '/',
        })
        reloadPage = true
      }

      // Reload the page to update content and remove parameters
      if (reloadPage) {
        window.location = origin
      }
    },
  },

  async mounted() {
    // Init data
    await this.initGeoCountry()
    this.initShop(this.geoCountry)

    jQuery(() => {
      // Handle ref parameters
      this.handleRefParams()

      // Check if modal can be shown
      this.canShow =
        !this.hasCookie() &&
        this.geoCountry &&
        this.shop &&
        this.shop.origin !== this.currentShopOrigin
    })
  },
})
</script>
</div>

<script data-ot-ignore type="text/javascript">
$(() => {
  let totalWIdth = 0;
  const $mobileShopHeaderSubmenuItems = $('#mobileShopHeaderSubmenu > li');
  $mobileShopHeaderSubmenuItems.each(function() { totalWIdth += $(this).width() });

  $('.comShopHeaderSubmenu .flexslider').flexslider({
    animation: 'slide',
    controlNav: false,
    animationLoop: false,
    slideshow: false,
    itemWidth: totalWIdth / $mobileShopHeaderSubmenuItems.length,
    itemMargin: 0,
    start: $slider => {
      const { pagingCount } = $slider;
      const itemIndex = $slider.find('.comShopHeaderSubmenu__item.active').index();
      const slidePageIndex = pagingCount !== 1 ? Math.floor(itemIndex / pagingCount) : 0;

      $slider.flexAnimate(slidePageIndex);
    },
  });
});
$(window).on('resize', () => {
  const flexData = jQuery('.comShopHeaderSubmenu .flexslider').data('flexslider');

  if (flexData) {
    flexData.setup();
  }
});
</script>

<div class="page__notes-container" id="notesApp">
    <template>
        <div class="comNote__wrapper clearfix" id="page__notes-wrapper" ref="comNote__wrapper" style="display: none;">
            <div class="comNote__wrapper-inner" ref="comNote__wrapperInner">
                <div class="comNote clearfix" :id="'comNote__' + note.uid" v-for="(note, i) in notes"><div class="text" v-html="note.textDefault"></div><a class="btn btn--simple" @click="hideNote(note.uid, 30, i)">Okay</a>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </template>
</div>

<script data-ot-ignore type="text/javascript">

    const NOTES_APP = new Vue({
        el: '#notesApp',

        delimiters: ['${', '}'],

        data() {
            return {
                apiUrl: '/apps/shop-manager/api/notes',
                notes: [],
                marginBottom: 16,
            }
        },


        mounted() {
            this.fetchNotes();
            window.addEventListener('resize', this.handleWrapperSize);
        },

        computed: {
            shopOrigin() {
                return window.Shopify.Checkout
                    ? window.Shopify.Checkout.apiHost
                    : window.Shopify.shop
            },
            hasNotes() {
                return this.notes.length !== 0;
            }
        },

        methods: {
            async fetchNotes() {
                const rawResponse = await fetch(`${this.apiUrl}?shop=${this.shopOrigin}`);
                const response = rawResponse.status === 200 && await rawResponse.json();
                const currentDate = new Date();
                let notes = [];

                if (response && response.success) {
                    response.data.forEach(note => {
                        let hide = false;

                        if (typeof $.cookie === 'function') {
                            const noteCookie = $.cookie('comNote__' + note.uid);

                            if (noteCookie && noteCookie.substring(0, 7) === 'clicked') {
                                let dateCookieCreated = noteCookie.substring(9, noteCookie.length);
                                dateCookieCreated = new Date(dateCookieCreated)

                                //delete cookie if note updateed
                                const deleteCookie = dateCookieCreated.getTime() <= new Date(note.updatedAt).getTime();
                                if (deleteCookie) {
                                    $.removeCookie('comNote__' + note.uid);
                                } else {
                                    hide = true;
                                }
                            }
                        }

                        if (!hide && note.active && (currentDate.getTime() <= new Date(note.endDate).getTime() && currentDate.getTime() >= new Date(note.startDate).getTime())) {
                            notes.push(note);
                        }
                    });
                }
                this.notes = notes;
            },
            showNote(element) {
                element.show();
                const $wrapperHeight = element.find('.comNote__wrapper-inner').outerHeight(true);

                element.animate({
                    height: $wrapperHeight + this.marginBottom
                }, 500);
            },
            hideNote(id, duration, index) {
                const $el = $('#comNote__' + id);
                const $noteHeight = $el.outerHeight(true)

                const $wrapper = $('#page__notes-wrapper');
                const $wrapperHeight = $wrapper.outerHeight(true);

                this.notes.splice(index, 1);

                $wrapper.animate({
                    height: $wrapperHeight - $noteHeight
                }, 500);

                const currentDate = new Date();
                $.cookie('comNote__' + id, 'clicked__' + currentDate.toISOString(), {
                    expires: duration,
                    path: '/'
                });
            },
            handleWrapperSize() {
                if (this.hasNotes) {
                    const wrapper = this.$refs.comNote__wrapper;
                    const wrapperRec = wrapper.getBoundingClientRect()
                    const innerWrapper = this.$refs.comNote__wrapperInner;
                    const innerWrapperRec = innerWrapper.getBoundingClientRect()

                    if (innerWrapperRec.height > (wrapperRec.height - this.marginBottom)) {
                        wrapper.style.height = innerWrapperRec.height + this.marginBottom + 'px';
                    } else if (innerWrapperRec.height < (wrapperRec.height - this.marginBottom)) {
                        wrapper.style.height = innerWrapperRec.height + this.marginBottom + 'px';
                    }
                }
            }
        },
        watch: {
            notes(notes) {
                if (notes.length !== 0) {
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        const el = $('#page__notes-wrapper');
                        this.showNote(el);
                    }, 500);
                }
            },
        },
    })
</script>
