<script>
  const carouselApp = {
    state: {
      currentSlide: 1,
      autoRotateInterval: null,
      autoRotateDirection: 'right',

      animationTimeout: null,
      isAnimating: false,
      touchstartX: 0,
      touchendX: 0,
    },

    elements: {
      container: document.getElementById('bannerCarousel_slidesContainer'),
      slides: document.getElementById('bannerCarousel_slides'),
      nav: document.getElementById('bannerCarousel_nav'),
      navRight: document.getElementById('bannerCarousel_navRight'),
      navLeft: document.getElementById('bannerCarousel_navLeft'),
      footer: document.getElementById('bannerCarousel_footer'),
    },

    // Get count of slides in carousel
    getSlidesCount() {
      return this.elements.slides.childElementCount
    },

    // Get width of the overflow container in carousel
    getContainerWidth() {
      return this.elements.container.getBoundingClientRect().width
    },

    handleGesture() {
      const { touchendX, touchstartX } = this.state
      const touchSlideDistance = (touchstartX - touchendX)

      if (touchSlideDistance < -50) {
        this.slideLeft(true)
      } else if (touchSlideDistance > 50) {
        this.slideRight(true)
      } else {
        this.slideTo(this.state.currentSlide, true)
      }
    },

    // Helper to slide one step left
    slideLeft(cancelInterval = false, clickEvent) {
      const { currentSlide } = this.state
      const { slides } = this.elements

      if (clickEvent && clickEvent.stopPropagation) {
        clickEvent.stopPropagation()
      }

      if (currentSlide > 1) {
        this.slideTo(currentSlide - 1, cancelInterval)
      } else {
        this.slideTo(currentSlide)
      }
    },

    // Helper to slide one step right
    slideRight(cancelInterval = false, clickEvent) {
      const { currentSlide } = this.state
      const { slides } = this.elements

      if (clickEvent && clickEvent.stopPropagation) {
        clickEvent.stopPropagation()
      }

      if (currentSlide < this.getSlidesCount()) {
        this.slideTo(currentSlide + 1, cancelInterval)
      } else {
        this.slideTo(currentSlide)
      }
    },

    // Slide to slide number - (index 1)
    slideTo(slideNum, cancelInterval = false) {
      clearInterval(this.state.animationTimeout)
      this.state.isAnimating = true

      this.state.animationTimeout = setTimeout(() => {
        this.state.isAnimating = false
      }, 800)

      if (cancelInterval) {
        clearInterval(this.state.autoRotateInterval)
      }

      const { navLeft, navRight } = this.elements

      if (slideNum === 1) {
        navLeft.classList.add('disabled')
      } else {
        navLeft.classList.remove('disabled')
      }

      if (slideNum === this.getSlidesCount()) {
        navRight.classList.add('disabled')
      } else {
        navRight.classList.remove('disabled')
      }

      this.state.currentSlide = slideNum

      const leftPos = this.getContainerWidth() * (slideNum - 1)
      this.elements.slides.style.left = `${-leftPos}px`

      this.updateActiveThumb()
    },

    // Set the static width of slides
    setSlidesWidth() {
      const { slides, container } = this.elements
      const containerWidth = this.getContainerWidth()

      this.slideTo(1)

      slides.style.width = `${containerWidth}px`
    },

    // Update thumb elements to show current active slide
    updateActiveThumb() {
      const { currentSlide } = this.state
      const { footer } = this.elements

      let i = 0
      for (const el of footer.children) {
        if (i + 1 === currentSlide) {
          el.classList.add('active')
        } else {
          el.classList.remove('active')
        }

        i += 1
      }
    },

    initSlideThumbs() {
      const { footer } = this.elements
      const indicatorHTML = `<svg width="9" height="8" viewBox="0 0 9 8" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><circle cx="4.5" cy="4" r="4" fill="#C8CAD3"/></svg>`

      for (let i = 0; i < this.getSlidesCount(); i++) {
        const el = document.createElement('button')

        el.innerHTML = indicatorHTML
        el.id = `bannerCarouselThumb_${i + 1}`
        el.classList.add('banner-carousel__thumb')

        el.addEventListener('click', () => {
          this.slideTo(i + 1, true)
        })

        footer.appendChild(el)
      }

      this.updateActiveThumb()
    },

    initInterval() {
      this.state.autoRotateInterval = setInterval(() => {
        const { currentSlide, autoRotateDirection } = this.state
        const slidesCount = this.getSlidesCount()

        if (autoRotateDirection === 'right' && currentSlide < slidesCount) {
          this.slideRight()
        } else if (autoRotateDirection === 'right') {
          this.state.autoRotateDirection = 'left'
          this.slideLeft()
        } else if (autoRotateDirection === 'left' && currentSlide > 1) {
          this.slideLeft()
        } else if (autoRotateDirection === 'left') {
          this.state.autoRotateDirection = 'right'
          this.slideRight()
        }
      }, 6000)
    },

    init() {
      const {
        container,
        slides,
        navRight,
        navLeft,
        nav,
      } = this.elements

      this.setSlidesWidth()
      this.initSlideThumbs()
      this.slideTo(1)
      this.initInterval()

      window.addEventListener('resize', this.setSlidesWidth.bind(this))
      navRight.addEventListener('click', () => this.slideRight.bind(this)(true, event))
      navLeft.addEventListener('click', () => this.slideLeft.bind(this)(true, event))

      /**
       * Record touchstart X positon
       */
      container.addEventListener('touchstart', e => {
        if (this.state.isAnimating) {
          this.state.touchstartX = null
          return
        }

        slides.style.transition = 'none'
        this.state.touchstartX = e.changedTouches[0].screenX
      })

      /**
       * Visual "drag" animation
       */
      container.addEventListener('touchmove', e => {
        if (typeof this.state.touchstartX !== 'number') {
          return
        }

        const draggedDistance = e.changedTouches[0].screenX - this.state.touchstartX
        const currentSlideLeftPos = 0 - (this.getContainerWidth() * (this.state.currentSlide - 1))

        const draggedLeftPos = currentSlideLeftPos + (draggedDistance / 2)
        const minLeftPos = 0 - (this.getContainerWidth() * (this.getSlidesCount() - 1))

        if (draggedLeftPos < 0 && draggedLeftPos > minLeftPos) {
          slides.style.left = `${draggedLeftPos}px`
        }
      })

      /**
       * Record touchend X positon and check if valid gesture for carousel slide
       */
      container.addEventListener('touchend', e => {
        if (typeof this.state.touchstartX !== 'number') {
          return
        }

        slides.style.transition = 'left .8s'
        this.state.touchendX = e.changedTouches[0].screenX
        this.handleGesture()
      })

      nav.style.display = 'block'
    },
  }

  window.addEventListener('load', () => {
    carouselApp.init()
  })
</script>

    <script type="text/javascript" src="//jp.store.ui.com/cdn/shop/t/6/assets/fastclick.min.js?v=179033935942447292241671553874"></script>
    <script type="text/javascript" src="//jp.store.ui.com/cdn/shop/t/6/assets/jquery.magnific-popup.min.js?v=36094560348524307761671553878"></script>
    <script type="text/javascript" src="//jp.store.ui.com/cdn/shop/t/6/assets/jquery.total-storage.min.js?v=139737745394735476471671553870"></script>
    <script type="text/javascript" src="//jp.store.ui.com/cdn/shop/t/6/assets/jquery.tablesorter.min.js?v=180626239223420059071608736805"></script>
    <script type="text/javascript" src="//jp.store.ui.com/cdn/shop/t/6/assets/videos.js?v=8455111029125680961671553895"></script>
    <script type="text/javascript" src="//jp.store.ui.com/cdn/shop/t/6/assets/froogaloop2.js?v=45102192857931299201671553879"></script>
    <script type="text/javascript" src="//jp.store.ui.com/cdn/shop/t/6/assets/timber.js?v=13884230966564342811692793074"></script>
    <script type="text/javascript" src="//jp.store.ui.com/cdn/shop/t/6/assets/search.js?v=117502843443102654421671553869"></script>
    <script>
  new Vue({
    el: '#header-mobile-menu',
  
    delimiters: ['${', '}'],
  
    data() {
      return {
        show: false,
        tmpScrollTop: 0,
        menuData: HEADER_MENU_DATA,
        selectedMenuItem: null,
      };
    },
  
    computed: {
      selectedMenuItemType() {
        let type = '';
  
        if (this.selectedMenuItem) {
          const { url } = this.selectedMenuItem;
  
          if (url.includes('unifi')) {
            type = 'unifi';
          } else if (url.includes('operator')) {
            type = 'operator';
          } else if (url.includes('early-access')) {
            type = 'beta';
          }
        }
  
        return type;
      },
  
      selectedMenuItemIndex() {
        if (this.selectedMenuItem) {
          const { title, url } = this.selectedMenuItem;
  
          switch (this.selectedMenuItemType) {
            case 'unifi':
              return this.menuData.unifi.findIndex(item => item.title === title && item.url === url);
  
            case 'operator':
              return this.menuData.operator.findIndex(item => item.title === title && item.url === url);
          }
        }
        return -1;
      },
  
      selectedMenuItemTitleContent() {
        const { operatorMenuImages } = this.menuData;
        let content = '';
  
        if (this.selectedMenuItem && operatorMenuImages) {
          const { title, url } = this.selectedMenuItem;
  
          switch (this.selectedMenuItemType) {
            case 'operator':
              // Set the SVG as the content
              content = operatorMenuImages[this.selectedMenuItemIndex];
              break;
  
            default:
              // Set the title by default
              content = title;
          }
        }
  
        return content;
      },
  
      activeMenuTitle() {
        let unifiItem = this.menuData.unifi.filter(item => {
          return item.active
        })
  
        // let operatorItem =  this.menuData.operator.filter(item => {
        //   return item.active
        // })
        
        if(unifiItem[0]) {
          return unifiItem[0].title
  
        // } else if(operatorItem[0]) {
        //   return operatorItem[0].title
  
        } else {
          return false
        }
      }
  
    },
  
    methods: {
      /**
       * @param {string?} prefix
       * @returns {string}
       */
      selectedMenuItemClass(prefix = '') {
        const className = this.selectedMenuItemType || 'default';
  
        return `${prefix}${className}`;
      },
  
      /**
       * @param {Event} e
       */
      toggleMenu(e) {
        e.preventDefault();
  
        this.show = !this.show;
      },
  
      adjustMenuStyle() {
        const headerEl = document.querySelector('.comGlobalHeader');
        const menuEl = this.$refs.menu;
  
        if (menuEl) {
          // menuEl.style.top = `${headerEl.offsetHeight}px`;
          menuEl.style.height = `${window.innerHeight - headerEl.offsetHeight}px`;
        }
      },
  
      /**
       * @param {Object} item
       */
      menuItemClick(item) {
        if (item.links.length) {
          // Set the item as active menu item
          this.selectedMenuItem = item;
        } else {
          // Navigate to the page
          window.location = item.url;
        }
      },
  
      /**
       * @param {Event} e
       */
      deselectMenuItem(e) {
        e.preventDefault();
  
        this.selectedMenuItem = null;
      },
  
      /**
       * Force hide the cart banner
       * Using direct element manipulation is a bad practice,
       * however, there is no state management yet to do it the right way
       *
       * @param {boolean} state
       */
      toggleCartBanner(state) {
        // Use the outer wrappper to not interfere with the main element styles
        const cartBannerEl = document.querySelector('.cartBanner__outer');
  
        if (cartBannerEl) {
          cartBannerEl.style.display = !state ? 'none' : 'block';
        }
      }
    },
  
    watch: {
      /**
       * @param {boolean} state
       */
      show(state) {
        if (state) {
          // Scroll to the top of the page
          jQuery('html, body').scrollTop(0);
  
          // Disable body scrolling
          this.tmpScrollTop = jQuery(window).scrollTop();
          jQuery('body').css('overflow', 'hidden');
  
          // Hide the banner
          this.toggleCartBanner(false);
        } else {
          // Enable body scrolling
          jQuery('body').css('overflow', 'auto');
          jQuery(window).scrollTop(this.tmpScrollTop);
  
          // Show the banner
          this.toggleCartBanner(true);
        }
      },
    },
  
    mounted() {
      // Body ready actions
      jQuery(() => {
        this.adjustMenuStyle();
      })
  
      // Events
      window.addEventListener('resize', this.adjustMenuStyle);
    },
  
    beforeDestroy() {
      window.removeEventListener('resize', this.adjustMenuStyle);
    },
  });
  </script>
  
  
</body>
</html>
